4501 assert(add.type().equals(intfn2));
4502 MethodHandle twice = permuteArguments(add, intfn1, 0, 0);
4503 assert(twice.type().equals(intfn1));
4504 assert((int)twice.invokeExact(21) == 42);
4505      * }</pre></blockquote>
4506      * <p>
4507      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
4508      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
4509      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are reordered
4510      * @param newType the expected type of the new method handle
4511      * @param reorder an index array which controls the reordering
4512      * @return a method handle which delegates to the target after it
4513      *           drops unused arguments and moves and/or duplicates the other arguments
4514      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
4515      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the index array length is not equal to
4516      *                  the arity of the target, or if any index array element
4517      *                  not a valid index for a parameter of {@code newType},
4518      *                  or if two corresponding parameter types in
4519      *                  {@code target.type()} and {@code newType} are not identical,
4520      */
4521     public static MethodHandle permuteArguments(MethodHandle target, MethodType newType, int... reorder) {
4522         reorder = reorder.clone();  // get a private copy
4523         MethodType oldType = target.type();
4524         permuteArgumentChecks(reorder, newType, oldType);
4525         // first detect dropped arguments and handle them separately
4526         int[] originalReorder = reorder;
4527         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
4528         LambdaForm form = result.form;
4529         int newArity = newType.parameterCount();
4530         // Normalize the reordering into a real permutation,
4531         // by removing duplicates and adding dropped elements.
4532         // This somewhat improves lambda form caching, as well
4533         // as simplifying the transform by breaking it up into steps.
4534         for (int ddIdx; (ddIdx = findFirstDupOrDrop(reorder, newArity)) != 0; ) {
4535             if (ddIdx > 0) {
4536                 // We found a duplicated entry at reorder[ddIdx].
4537                 // Example:  (x,y,z)->asList(x,y,z)
4538                 // permuted by [1*,0,1] => (a0,a1)=>asList(a1,a0,a1)
4539                 // permuted by [0,1,0*] => (a0,a1)=>asList(a0,a1,a0)
4540                 // The starred element corresponds to the argument
4541                 // deleted by the dupArgumentForm transform.
4542                 int srcPos = ddIdx, dstPos = srcPos, dupVal = reorder[srcPos];
4543                 boolean killFirst = false;
4544                 for (int val; (val = reorder[--dstPos]) != dupVal; ) {
4545                     // Set killFirst if the dup is larger than an intervening position.
4546                     // This will remove at least one inversion from the permutation.
4547                     if (dupVal > val) killFirst = true;
4548                 }
4549                 if (!killFirst) {
4550                     srcPos = dstPos;
4551                     dstPos = ddIdx;
4552                 }
4553                 form = form.editor().dupArgumentForm(1 + srcPos, 1 + dstPos);
4554                 assert (reorder[srcPos] == reorder[dstPos]);
4555                 oldType = oldType.dropParameterTypes(dstPos, dstPos + 1);
4556                 // contract the reordering by removing the element at dstPos
4557                 int tailPos = dstPos + 1;
4558                 System.arraycopy(reorder, tailPos, reorder, dstPos, reorder.length - tailPos);
4559                 reorder = Arrays.copyOf(reorder, reorder.length - 1);
4560             } else {
4561                 int dropVal = ~ddIdx, insPos = 0;
4562                 while (insPos < reorder.length && reorder[insPos] < dropVal) {
4563                     // Find first element of reorder larger than dropVal.
4564                     // This is where we will insert the dropVal.
4565                     insPos += 1;
4566                 }
4567                 Class<?> ptype = newType.parameterType(dropVal);
4568                 form = form.editor().addArgumentForm(1 + insPos, BasicType.basicType(ptype));
4569                 oldType = oldType.insertParameterTypes(insPos, ptype);
4570                 // expand the reordering by inserting an element at insPos
4571                 int tailPos = insPos + 1;
4572                 reorder = Arrays.copyOf(reorder, reorder.length + 1);
4573                 System.arraycopy(reorder, insPos, reorder, tailPos, reorder.length - tailPos);
4574                 reorder[insPos] = dropVal;
4575             }
4576             assert (permuteArgumentChecks(reorder, newType, oldType));
4577         }
4578         assert (reorder.length == newArity);  // a perfect permutation
4579         // Note:  This may cache too many distinct LFs. Consider backing off to varargs code.
4580         form = form.editor().permuteArgumentsForm(1, reorder);
4581         if (newType == result.type() && form == result.internalForm())
4582             return result;
4583         return result.copyWith(newType, form);
4584     }
4585 
4586     /**
4587      * Return an indication of any duplicate or omission in reorder.
4588      * If the reorder contains a duplicate entry, return the index of the second occurrence.
4589      * Otherwise, return ~(n), for the first n in [0..newArity-1] that is not present in reorder.
4590      * Otherwise, return zero.
4591      * If an element not in [0..newArity-1] is encountered, return reorder.length.
4592      */
4593     private static int findFirstDupOrDrop(int[] reorder, int newArity) {
4594         final int BIT_LIMIT = 63;  // max number of bits in bit mask
4595         if (newArity < BIT_LIMIT) {
4596             long mask = 0;
4597             for (int i = 0; i < reorder.length; i++) {
4598                 int arg = reorder[i];
4599                 if (arg >= newArity) {
4600                     return reorder.length;
4601                 }
4602                 long bit = 1L << arg;
4603                 if ((mask & bit) != 0) {
4604                     return i;  // >0 indicates a dup
4605                 }
4606                 mask |= bit;
4607             }
4608             if (mask == (1L << newArity) - 1) {
4609                 assert(Long.numberOfTrailingZeros(Long.lowestOneBit(~mask)) == newArity);
4610                 return 0;
4611             }
4612             // find first zero
4613             long zeroBit = Long.lowestOneBit(~mask);
4614             int zeroPos = Long.numberOfTrailingZeros(zeroBit);
4615             assert(zeroPos <= newArity);
4616             if (zeroPos == newArity) {
4617                 return 0;
4618             }
4619             return ~zeroPos;
4620         } else {
4621             // same algorithm, different bit set
4622             BitSet mask = new BitSet(newArity);
4623             for (int i = 0; i < reorder.length; i++) {
4624                 int arg = reorder[i];
4625                 if (arg >= newArity) {
4626                     return reorder.length;
4627                 }
4628                 if (mask.get(arg)) {
4629                     return i;  // >0 indicates a dup
4630                 }
4631                 mask.set(arg);
4632             }
4633             int zeroPos = mask.nextClearBit(0);
4634             assert(zeroPos <= newArity);
4635             if (zeroPos == newArity) {
4636                 return 0;
4637             }
4638             return ~zeroPos;
4639         }
4640     }
4641 
4642     private static boolean permuteArgumentChecks(int[] reorder, MethodType newType, MethodType oldType) {
4643         if (newType.returnType() != oldType.returnType())
4644             throw newIllegalArgumentException("return types do not match",
4645                     oldType, newType);
4646         if (reorder.length == oldType.parameterCount()) {
4647             int limit = newType.parameterCount();
4648             boolean bad = false;
4649             for (int j = 0; j < reorder.length; j++) {
4650                 int i = reorder[j];
4651                 if (i < 0 || i >= limit) {
4652                     bad = true; break;
4653                 }
4654                 Class<?> src = newType.parameterType(i);
4655                 Class<?> dst = oldType.parameterType(j);
4656                 if (src != dst)
4657                     throw newIllegalArgumentException("parameter types do not match after reorder",
4658                             oldType, newType);
4659             }
4660             if (!bad)  return true;
4661         }
4662         throw newIllegalArgumentException("bad reorder array: "+Arrays.toString(reorder));
4663     }
4664 
4665     /**
4666      * Produces a method handle of the requested return type which returns the given
4667      * constant value every time it is invoked.
4668      * <p>
4669      * Before the method handle is returned, the passed-in value is converted to the requested type.
4670      * If the requested type is primitive, widening primitive conversions are attempted,
4671      * else reference conversions are attempted.
4672      * <p>The returned method handle is equivalent to {@code identity(type).bindTo(value)}.
4673      * @param type the return type of the desired method handle
4674      * @param value the value to return
4675      * @return a method handle of the given return type and no arguments, which always returns the given value
4676      * @throws NullPointerException if the {@code type} argument is null
4677      * @throws ClassCastException if the value cannot be converted to the required return type
4678      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the given type is {@code void.class}
4679      */
4680     public static MethodHandle constant(Class<?> type, Object value) {
4681         if (type.isPrimitive()) {
4682             if (type == void.class)
4683                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("void type");
4684             Wrapper w = Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(type);
4685             value = w.convert(value, type);
4686             if (w.zero().equals(value))
4687                 return zero(w, type);
4688             return insertArguments(identity(type), 0, value);
4689         } else {
4690             if (value == null)
4691                 return zero(Wrapper.OBJECT, type);
4692             return identity(type).bindTo(value);
4693         }
4694     }
4695 
4696     /**
4697      * Produces a method handle which returns its sole argument when invoked.
4698      * @param type the type of the sole parameter and return value of the desired method handle
4699      * @return a unary method handle which accepts and returns the given type
4700      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
4701      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the given type is {@code void.class}
4702      */
4703     public static MethodHandle identity(Class<?> type) {
4704         Wrapper btw = (type.isPrimitive() ? Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(type) : Wrapper.OBJECT);
4705         int pos = btw.ordinal();
4706         MethodHandle ident = IDENTITY_MHS[pos];
4707         if (ident == null) {
4708             ident = setCachedMethodHandle(IDENTITY_MHS, pos, makeIdentity(btw.primitiveType()));
4709         }
4710         if (ident.type().returnType() == type)
4711             return ident;
4712         // something like identity(Foo.class); do not bother to intern these
4713         assert (btw == Wrapper.OBJECT);
4714         return makeIdentity(type);
4715     }
4716 
4717     /**
4718      * Produces a constant method handle of the requested return type which
4719      * returns the default value for that type every time it is invoked.
4720      * The resulting constant method handle will have no side effects.
4721      * <p>The returned method handle is equivalent to {@code empty(methodType(type))}.
4722      * It is also equivalent to {@code explicitCastArguments(constant(Object.class, null), methodType(type))},
4723      * since {@code explicitCastArguments} converts {@code null} to default values.
4724      * @param type the expected return type of the desired method handle
4725      * @return a constant method handle that takes no arguments
4726      *         and returns the default value of the given type (or void, if the type is void)
4727      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
4728      * @see MethodHandles#constant
4729      * @see MethodHandles#empty
4730      * @see MethodHandles#explicitCastArguments
4731      * @since 9
4732      */
4733     public static MethodHandle zero(Class<?> type) {
4734         Objects.requireNonNull(type);
4735         if (type.isPrimitive()) {
4736             return zero(Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(type), type);
4737         } else if (type.isInlineClass()) {
4738             throw new UnsupportedOperationException();
4739         } else {
4740             return zero(Wrapper.OBJECT, type);
4741         }
4742     }
4743 
4744     private static MethodHandle identityOrVoid(Class<?> type) {
4745         return type == void.class ? zero(type) : identity(type);
4746     }
4747 
4748     /**
4749      * Produces a method handle of the requested type which ignores any arguments, does nothing,
4750      * and returns a suitable default depending on the return type.
4751      * That is, it returns a zero primitive value, a {@code null}, or {@code void}.
4752      * <p>The returned method handle is equivalent to
4753      * {@code dropArguments(zero(type.returnType()), 0, type.parameterList())}.
4754      *
4755      * @apiNote Given a predicate and target, a useful "if-then" construct can be produced as
4756      * {@code guardWithTest(pred, target, empty(target.type())}.
4757      * @param type the type of the desired method handle
4758      * @return a constant method handle of the given type, which returns a default value of the given return type
4759      * @throws NullPointerException if the argument is null
4760      * @see MethodHandles#zero
4761      * @see MethodHandles#constant
4762      * @since 9
4763      */
4764     public static  MethodHandle empty(MethodType type) {
4765         Objects.requireNonNull(type);
4766         return dropArguments(zero(type.returnType()), 0, type.parameterList());
4767     }
4768 
4769     private static final MethodHandle[] IDENTITY_MHS = new MethodHandle[Wrapper.COUNT];
4770     private static MethodHandle makeIdentity(Class<?> ptype) {
4771         MethodType mtype = MethodType.methodType(ptype, ptype);
4772         LambdaForm lform = LambdaForm.identityForm(BasicType.basicType(ptype));
4773         return MethodHandleImpl.makeIntrinsic(mtype, lform, Intrinsic.IDENTITY);
4774     }
4775 
4776     private static MethodHandle zero(Wrapper btw, Class<?> rtype) {
4777         int pos = btw.ordinal();
4778         MethodHandle zero = ZERO_MHS[pos];
4779         if (zero == null) {
4780             zero = setCachedMethodHandle(ZERO_MHS, pos, makeZero(btw.primitiveType()));
4781         }
4782         if (zero.type().returnType() == rtype)
4783             return zero;
4784         assert(btw == Wrapper.OBJECT);
4785         return makeZero(rtype);
4786     }
4787     private static final MethodHandle[] ZERO_MHS = new MethodHandle[Wrapper.COUNT];
4788     private static MethodHandle makeZero(Class<?> rtype) {
4789         MethodType mtype = methodType(rtype);
4790         LambdaForm lform = LambdaForm.zeroForm(BasicType.basicType(rtype));
4791         return MethodHandleImpl.makeIntrinsic(mtype, lform, Intrinsic.ZERO);
4792     }
4793 
4794     private static synchronized MethodHandle setCachedMethodHandle(MethodHandle[] cache, int pos, MethodHandle value) {
4795         // Simulate a CAS, to avoid racy duplication of results.
4796         MethodHandle prev = cache[pos];
4797         if (prev != null) return prev;
4798         return cache[pos] = value;
4799     }
4800 
4801     /**
4802      * Provides a target method handle with one or more <em>bound arguments</em>
4803      * in advance of the method handle's invocation.
4804      * The formal parameters to the target corresponding to the bound
4805      * arguments are called <em>bound parameters</em>.
4806      * Returns a new method handle which saves away the bound arguments.
4807      * When it is invoked, it receives arguments for any non-bound parameters,
4808      * binds the saved arguments to their corresponding parameters,
4809      * and calls the original target.
4810      * <p>
4811      * The type of the new method handle will drop the types for the bound
4812      * parameters from the original target type, since the new method handle
4813      * will no longer require those arguments to be supplied by its callers.
4814      * <p>
4815      * Each given argument object must match the corresponding bound parameter type.
4816      * If a bound parameter type is a primitive, the argument object
4817      * must be a wrapper, and will be unboxed to produce the primitive value.
4818      * <p>
4819      * The {@code pos} argument selects which parameters are to be bound.
4820      * It may range between zero and <i>N-L</i> (inclusively),
4821      * where <i>N</i> is the arity of the target method handle
4822      * and <i>L</i> is the length of the values array.
4823      * <p>
4824      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
4825      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
4826      * @param target the method handle to invoke after the argument is inserted
4827      * @param pos where to insert the argument (zero for the first)
4828      * @param values the series of arguments to insert
4829      * @return a method handle which inserts an additional argument,
4830      *         before calling the original method handle
4831      * @throws NullPointerException if the target or the {@code values} array is null
4832      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if (@code pos) is less than {@code 0} or greater than
4833      *         {@code N - L} where {@code N} is the arity of the target method handle and {@code L}
4834      *         is the length of the values array.
4835      * @throws ClassCastException if an argument does not match the corresponding bound parameter
4836      *         type.
4837      * @see MethodHandle#bindTo
4838      */
4839     public static MethodHandle insertArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, Object... values) {
4840         int insCount = values.length;
4841         Class<?>[] ptypes = insertArgumentsChecks(target, insCount, pos);
4842         if (insCount == 0)  return target;
4843         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
4844         for (int i = 0; i < insCount; i++) {
4845             Object value = values[i];
4846             Class<?> ptype = ptypes[pos+i];
4847             if (ptype.isPrimitive()) {
4848                 result = insertArgumentPrimitive(result, pos, ptype, value);
4849             } else {
4850                 value = ptype.cast(value);  // throw CCE if needed
4851                 result = result.bindArgumentL(pos, value);
4852             }
4853         }
4854         return result;
4855     }
4856 
4857     private static BoundMethodHandle insertArgumentPrimitive(BoundMethodHandle result, int pos,
4858                                                              Class<?> ptype, Object value) {
4859         Wrapper w = Wrapper.forPrimitiveType(ptype);
4860         // perform unboxing and/or primitive conversion
4861         value = w.convert(value, ptype);
4862         switch (w) {
4863         case INT:     return result.bindArgumentI(pos, (int)value);
4864         case LONG:    return result.bindArgumentJ(pos, (long)value);
4865         case FLOAT:   return result.bindArgumentF(pos, (float)value);
4866         case DOUBLE:  return result.bindArgumentD(pos, (double)value);
4867         default:      return result.bindArgumentI(pos, ValueConversions.widenSubword(value));
4868         }
4869     }
4870 
4871     private static Class<?>[] insertArgumentsChecks(MethodHandle target, int insCount, int pos) throws RuntimeException {
4872         MethodType oldType = target.type();
4873         int outargs = oldType.parameterCount();
4874         int inargs  = outargs - insCount;
4875         if (inargs < 0)
4876             throw newIllegalArgumentException("too many values to insert");
4877         if (pos < 0 || pos > inargs)
4878             throw newIllegalArgumentException("no argument type to append");
4879         return oldType.ptypes();
4880     }
4881 
4882     /**
4883      * Produces a method handle which will discard some dummy arguments
4884      * before calling some other specified <i>target</i> method handle.
4885      * The type of the new method handle will be the same as the target's type,
4886      * except it will also include the dummy argument types,
4887      * at some given position.
4888      * <p>
4889      * The {@code pos} argument may range between zero and <i>N</i>,
4890      * where <i>N</i> is the arity of the target.
4891      * If {@code pos} is zero, the dummy arguments will precede
4892      * the target's real arguments; if {@code pos} is <i>N</i>
4893      * they will come after.
4894      * <p>
4895      * <b>Example:</b>
4896      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
4897 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
4898 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
4899 ...
4900 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
4901   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
4902 assertEquals("xy", (String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y"));
4903 MethodType bigType = cat.type().insertParameterTypes(0, int.class, String.class);
4904 MethodHandle d0 = dropArguments(cat, 0, bigType.parameterList().subList(0,2));
4905 assertEquals(bigType, d0.type());
4906 assertEquals("yz", (String) d0.invokeExact(123, "x", "y", "z"));
4907      * }</pre></blockquote>
4908      * <p>
4909      * This method is also equivalent to the following code:
4910      * <blockquote><pre>
4911      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle,int,Class...) dropArguments}{@code (target, pos, valueTypes.toArray(new Class[0]))}
4912      * </pre></blockquote>
4913      * @param target the method handle to invoke after the arguments are dropped
4914      * @param pos position of first argument to drop (zero for the leftmost)
4915      * @param valueTypes the type(s) of the argument(s) to drop
4916      * @return a method handle which drops arguments of the given types,
4917      *         before calling the original method handle
4918      * @throws NullPointerException if the target is null,
4919      *                              or if the {@code valueTypes} list or any of its elements is null
4920      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if any element of {@code valueTypes} is {@code void.class},
4921      *                  or if {@code pos} is negative or greater than the arity of the target,
4922      *                  or if the new method handle's type would have too many parameters
4923      */
4924     public static MethodHandle dropArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, List<Class<?>> valueTypes) {
4925         return dropArguments0(target, pos, copyTypes(valueTypes.toArray()));
4926     }
4927 
4928     private static List<Class<?>> copyTypes(Object[] array) {
4929         return Arrays.asList(Arrays.copyOf(array, array.length, Class[].class));
4930     }
4931 
4932     private static MethodHandle dropArguments0(MethodHandle target, int pos, List<Class<?>> valueTypes) {
4933         MethodType oldType = target.type();  // get NPE
4934         int dropped = dropArgumentChecks(oldType, pos, valueTypes);
4935         MethodType newType = oldType.insertParameterTypes(pos, valueTypes);
4936         if (dropped == 0)  return target;
4937         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
4938         LambdaForm lform = result.form;
4939         int insertFormArg = 1 + pos;
4940         for (Class<?> ptype : valueTypes) {
4941             lform = lform.editor().addArgumentForm(insertFormArg++, BasicType.basicType(ptype));
4942         }
4943         result = result.copyWith(newType, lform);
4944         return result;
4945     }
4946 
4947     private static int dropArgumentChecks(MethodType oldType, int pos, List<Class<?>> valueTypes) {
4948         int dropped = valueTypes.size();
4949         MethodType.checkSlotCount(dropped);
4950         int outargs = oldType.parameterCount();
4951         int inargs  = outargs + dropped;
4952         if (pos < 0 || pos > outargs)
4953             throw newIllegalArgumentException("no argument type to remove"
4954                     + Arrays.asList(oldType, pos, valueTypes, inargs, outargs)
4955                     );
4956         return dropped;
4957     }
4958 
4959     /**
4960      * Produces a method handle which will discard some dummy arguments
4961      * before calling some other specified <i>target</i> method handle.
4962      * The type of the new method handle will be the same as the target's type,
4963      * except it will also include the dummy argument types,
4964      * at some given position.
4965      * <p>
4966      * The {@code pos} argument may range between zero and <i>N</i>,
4967      * where <i>N</i> is the arity of the target.
4968      * If {@code pos} is zero, the dummy arguments will precede
4969      * the target's real arguments; if {@code pos} is <i>N</i>
4970      * they will come after.
4971      * @apiNote
4972      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
4973 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
4974 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
4975 ...
4976 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
4977   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
4978 assertEquals("xy", (String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y"));
4979 MethodHandle d0 = dropArguments(cat, 0, String.class);
4980 assertEquals("yz", (String) d0.invokeExact("x", "y", "z"));
4981 MethodHandle d1 = dropArguments(cat, 1, String.class);
4982 assertEquals("xz", (String) d1.invokeExact("x", "y", "z"));
4983 MethodHandle d2 = dropArguments(cat, 2, String.class);
4984 assertEquals("xy", (String) d2.invokeExact("x", "y", "z"));
4985 MethodHandle d12 = dropArguments(cat, 1, int.class, boolean.class);
4986 assertEquals("xz", (String) d12.invokeExact("x", 12, true, "z"));
4987      * }</pre></blockquote>
4988      * <p>
4989      * This method is also equivalent to the following code:
4990      * <blockquote><pre>
4991      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle,int,List) dropArguments}{@code (target, pos, Arrays.asList(valueTypes))}
4992      * </pre></blockquote>
4993      * @param target the method handle to invoke after the arguments are dropped
4994      * @param pos position of first argument to drop (zero for the leftmost)
4995      * @param valueTypes the type(s) of the argument(s) to drop
4996      * @return a method handle which drops arguments of the given types,
4997      *         before calling the original method handle
4998      * @throws NullPointerException if the target is null,
4999      *                              or if the {@code valueTypes} array or any of its elements is null
5000      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if any element of {@code valueTypes} is {@code void.class},
5001      *                  or if {@code pos} is negative or greater than the arity of the target,
5002      *                  or if the new method handle's type would have
5003      *                  <a href="MethodHandle.html#maxarity">too many parameters</a>
5004      */
5005     public static MethodHandle dropArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, Class<?>... valueTypes) {
5006         return dropArguments0(target, pos, copyTypes(valueTypes));
5007     }
5008 
5009     // private version which allows caller some freedom with error handling
5010     private static MethodHandle dropArgumentsToMatch(MethodHandle target, int skip, List<Class<?>> newTypes, int pos,
5011                                       boolean nullOnFailure) {
5012         newTypes = copyTypes(newTypes.toArray());
5013         List<Class<?>> oldTypes = target.type().parameterList();
5014         int match = oldTypes.size();
5015         if (skip != 0) {
5016             if (skip < 0 || skip > match) {
5017                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("illegal skip", skip, target);
5018             }
5019             oldTypes = oldTypes.subList(skip, match);
5020             match -= skip;
5021         }
5022         List<Class<?>> addTypes = newTypes;
5023         int add = addTypes.size();
5024         if (pos != 0) {
5025             if (pos < 0 || pos > add) {
5026                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("illegal pos", pos, newTypes);
5027             }
5028             addTypes = addTypes.subList(pos, add);
5029             add -= pos;
5030             assert(addTypes.size() == add);
5031         }
5032         // Do not add types which already match the existing arguments.
5033         if (match > add || !oldTypes.equals(addTypes.subList(0, match))) {
5034             if (nullOnFailure) {
5035                 return null;
5036             }
5037             throw newIllegalArgumentException("argument lists do not match", oldTypes, newTypes);
5038         }
5039         addTypes = addTypes.subList(match, add);
5040         add -= match;
5041         assert(addTypes.size() == add);
5042         // newTypes:     (   P*[pos], M*[match], A*[add] )
5043         // target: ( S*[skip],        M*[match]  )
5044         MethodHandle adapter = target;
5045         if (add > 0) {
5046             adapter = dropArguments0(adapter, skip+ match, addTypes);
5047         }
5048         // adapter: (S*[skip],        M*[match], A*[add] )
5049         if (pos > 0) {
5050             adapter = dropArguments0(adapter, skip, newTypes.subList(0, pos));
5051         }
5052         // adapter: (S*[skip], P*[pos], M*[match], A*[add] )
5053         return adapter;
5054     }
5055 
5056     /**
5057      * Adapts a target method handle to match the given parameter type list. If necessary, adds dummy arguments. Some
5058      * leading parameters can be skipped before matching begins. The remaining types in the {@code target}'s parameter
5059      * type list must be a sub-list of the {@code newTypes} type list at the starting position {@code pos}. The
5060      * resulting handle will have the target handle's parameter type list, with any non-matching parameter types (before
5061      * or after the matching sub-list) inserted in corresponding positions of the target's original parameters, as if by
5062      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle, int, Class[])}.
5063      * <p>
5064      * The resulting handle will have the same return type as the target handle.
5065      * <p>
5066      * In more formal terms, assume these two type lists:<ul>
5067      * <li>The target handle has the parameter type list {@code S..., M...}, with as many types in {@code S} as
5068      * indicated by {@code skip}. The {@code M} types are those that are supposed to match part of the given type list,
5069      * {@code newTypes}.
5070      * <li>The {@code newTypes} list contains types {@code P..., M..., A...}, with as many types in {@code P} as
5071      * indicated by {@code pos}. The {@code M} types are precisely those that the {@code M} types in the target handle's
5072      * parameter type list are supposed to match. The types in {@code A} are additional types found after the matching
5073      * sub-list.
5074      * </ul>
5075      * Given these assumptions, the result of an invocation of {@code dropArgumentsToMatch} will have the parameter type
5076      * list {@code S..., P..., M..., A...}, with the {@code P} and {@code A} types inserted as if by
5077      * {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle, int, Class[])}.
5078      *
5079      * @apiNote
5080      * Two method handles whose argument lists are "effectively identical" (i.e., identical in a common prefix) may be
5081      * mutually converted to a common type by two calls to {@code dropArgumentsToMatch}, as follows:
5082      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5083 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5084 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5085 ...
5086 ...
5087 MethodHandle h0 = constant(boolean.class, true);
5088 MethodHandle h1 = lookup().findVirtual(String.class, "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5089 MethodType bigType = h1.type().insertParameterTypes(1, String.class, int.class);
5090 MethodHandle h2 = dropArguments(h1, 0, bigType.parameterList());
5091 if (h1.type().parameterCount() < h2.type().parameterCount())
5092     h1 = dropArgumentsToMatch(h1, 0, h2.type().parameterList(), 0);  // lengthen h1
5093 else
5094     h2 = dropArgumentsToMatch(h2, 0, h1.type().parameterList(), 0);    // lengthen h2
5095 MethodHandle h3 = guardWithTest(h0, h1, h2);
5096 assertEquals("xy", h3.invoke("x", "y", 1, "a", "b", "c"));
5097      * }</pre></blockquote>
5098      * @param target the method handle to adapt
5099      * @param skip number of targets parameters to disregard (they will be unchanged)
5100      * @param newTypes the list of types to match {@code target}'s parameter type list to
5101      * @param pos place in {@code newTypes} where the non-skipped target parameters must occur
5102      * @return a possibly adapted method handle
5103      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5104      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if any element of {@code newTypes} is {@code void.class},
5105      *         or if {@code skip} is negative or greater than the arity of the target,
5106      *         or if {@code pos} is negative or greater than the newTypes list size,
5107      *         or if {@code newTypes} does not contain the {@code target}'s non-skipped parameter types at position
5108      *         {@code pos}.
5109      * @since 9
5110      */
5111     public static MethodHandle dropArgumentsToMatch(MethodHandle target, int skip, List<Class<?>> newTypes, int pos) {
5112         Objects.requireNonNull(target);
5113         Objects.requireNonNull(newTypes);
5114         return dropArgumentsToMatch(target, skip, newTypes, pos, false);
5115     }
5116 
5117     /**
5118      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing
5119      * one or more of its arguments, each with its own unary filter function,
5120      * and then calling the target with each pre-processed argument
5121      * replaced by the result of its corresponding filter function.
5122      * <p>
5123      * The pre-processing is performed by one or more method handles,
5124      * specified in the elements of the {@code filters} array.
5125      * The first element of the filter array corresponds to the {@code pos}
5126      * argument of the target, and so on in sequence.
5127      * The filter functions are invoked in left to right order.
5128      * <p>
5129      * Null arguments in the array are treated as identity functions,
5130      * and the corresponding arguments left unchanged.
5131      * (If there are no non-null elements in the array, the original target is returned.)
5132      * Each filter is applied to the corresponding argument of the adapter.
5133      * <p>
5134      * If a filter {@code F} applies to the {@code N}th argument of
5135      * the target, then {@code F} must be a method handle which
5136      * takes exactly one argument.  The type of {@code F}'s sole argument
5137      * replaces the corresponding argument type of the target
5138      * in the resulting adapted method handle.
5139      * The return type of {@code F} must be identical to the corresponding
5140      * parameter type of the target.
5141      * <p>
5142      * It is an error if there are elements of {@code filters}
5143      * (null or not)
5144      * which do not correspond to argument positions in the target.
5145      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5146      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5147 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5148 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5149 ...
5150 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5151   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5152 MethodHandle upcase = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5153   "toUpperCase", methodType(String.class));
5154 assertEquals("xy", (String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y"));
5155 MethodHandle f0 = filterArguments(cat, 0, upcase);
5156 assertEquals("Xy", (String) f0.invokeExact("x", "y")); // Xy
5157 MethodHandle f1 = filterArguments(cat, 1, upcase);
5158 assertEquals("xY", (String) f1.invokeExact("x", "y")); // xY
5159 MethodHandle f2 = filterArguments(cat, 0, upcase, upcase);
5160 assertEquals("XY", (String) f2.invokeExact("x", "y")); // XY
5161      * }</pre></blockquote>
5162      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5163      * denotes the return type of both the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5164      * {@code P}/{@code p} and {@code B}/{@code b} represent the types and values
5165      * of the parameters and arguments that precede and follow the filter position
5166      * {@code pos}, respectively. {@code A[i]}/{@code a[i]} stand for the types and
5167      * values of the filtered parameters and arguments; they also represent the
5168      * return types of the {@code filter[i]} handles. The latter accept arguments
5169      * {@code v[i]} of type {@code V[i]}, which also appear in the signature of
5170      * the resulting adapter.
5171      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5172      * T target(P... p, A[i]... a[i], B... b);
5173      * A[i] filter[i](V[i]);
5174      * T adapter(P... p, V[i]... v[i], B... b) {
5175      *   return target(p..., filter[i](v[i])..., b...);
5176      * }
5177      * }</pre></blockquote>
5178      * <p>
5179      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5180      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5181      *
5182      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are filtered
5183      * @param pos the position of the first argument to filter
5184      * @param filters method handles to call initially on filtered arguments
5185      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument filtering logic
5186      * @throws NullPointerException if the target is null
5187      *                              or if the {@code filters} array is null
5188      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if a non-null element of {@code filters}
5189      *          does not match a corresponding argument type of target as described above,
5190      *          or if the {@code pos+filters.length} is greater than {@code target.type().parameterCount()},
5191      *          or if the resulting method handle's type would have
5192      *          <a href="MethodHandle.html#maxarity">too many parameters</a>
5193      */
5194     public static MethodHandle filterArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle... filters) {
5195         // In method types arguments start at index 0, while the LF
5196         // editor have the MH receiver at position 0 - adjust appropriately.
5197         final int MH_RECEIVER_OFFSET = 1;
5198         filterArgumentsCheckArity(target, pos, filters);
5199         MethodHandle adapter = target;
5200 
5201         // keep track of currently matched filters, as to optimize repeated filters
5202         int index = 0;
5203         int[] positions = new int[filters.length];
5204         MethodHandle filter = null;
5205 
5206         // process filters in reverse order so that the invocation of
5207         // the resulting adapter will invoke the filters in left-to-right order
5208         for (int i = filters.length - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
5209             MethodHandle newFilter = filters[i];
5210             if (newFilter == null) continue;  // ignore null elements of filters
5211 
5212             // flush changes on update
5213             if (filter != newFilter) {
5214                 if (filter != null) {
5215                     if (index > 1) {
5216                         adapter = filterRepeatedArgument(adapter, filter, Arrays.copyOf(positions, index));
5217                     } else {
5218                         adapter = filterArgument(adapter, positions[0] - 1, filter);
5219                     }
5220                 }
5221                 filter = newFilter;
5222                 index = 0;
5223             }
5224 
5225             filterArgumentChecks(target, pos + i, newFilter);
5226             positions[index++] = pos + i + MH_RECEIVER_OFFSET;
5227         }
5228         if (index > 1) {
5229             adapter = filterRepeatedArgument(adapter, filter, Arrays.copyOf(positions, index));
5230         } else if (index == 1) {
5231             adapter = filterArgument(adapter, positions[0] - 1, filter);
5232         }
5233         return adapter;
5234     }
5235 
5236     private static MethodHandle filterRepeatedArgument(MethodHandle adapter, MethodHandle filter, int[] positions) {
5237         MethodType targetType = adapter.type();
5238         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5239         BoundMethodHandle result = adapter.rebind();
5240         Class<?> newParamType = filterType.parameterType(0);
5241 
5242         Class<?>[] ptypes = targetType.ptypes().clone();
5243         for (int pos : positions) {
5244             ptypes[pos - 1] = newParamType;
5245         }
5246         MethodType newType = MethodType.makeImpl(targetType.rtype(), ptypes, true);
5247 
5248         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().filterRepeatedArgumentForm(BasicType.basicType(newParamType), positions);
5249         return result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5250     }
5251 
5252     /*non-public*/
5253     static MethodHandle filterArgument(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) {
5254         filterArgumentChecks(target, pos, filter);
5255         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5256         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5257         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5258         Class<?> newParamType = filterType.parameterType(0);
5259         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().filterArgumentForm(1 + pos, BasicType.basicType(newParamType));
5260         MethodType newType = targetType.changeParameterType(pos, newParamType);
5261         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5262         return result;
5263     }
5264 
5265     private static void filterArgumentsCheckArity(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle[] filters) {
5266         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5267         int maxPos = targetType.parameterCount();
5268         if (pos + filters.length > maxPos)
5269             throw newIllegalArgumentException("too many filters");
5270     }
5271 
5272     private static void filterArgumentChecks(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) throws RuntimeException {
5273         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5274         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5275         if (filterType.parameterCount() != 1
5276             || filterType.returnType() != targetType.parameterType(pos))
5277             throw newIllegalArgumentException("target and filter types do not match", targetType, filterType);
5278     }
5279 
5280     /**
5281      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing
5282      * a sub-sequence of its arguments with a filter (another method handle).
5283      * The pre-processed arguments are replaced by the result (if any) of the
5284      * filter function.
5285      * The target is then called on the modified (usually shortened) argument list.
5286      * <p>
5287      * If the filter returns a value, the target must accept that value as
5288      * its argument in position {@code pos}, preceded and/or followed by
5289      * any arguments not passed to the filter.
5290      * If the filter returns void, the target must accept all arguments
5291      * not passed to the filter.
5292      * No arguments are reordered, and a result returned from the filter
5293      * replaces (in order) the whole subsequence of arguments originally
5294      * passed to the adapter.
5295      * <p>
5296      * The argument types (if any) of the filter
5297      * replace zero or one argument types of the target, at position {@code pos},
5298      * in the resulting adapted method handle.
5299      * The return type of the filter (if any) must be identical to the
5300      * argument type of the target at position {@code pos}, and that target argument
5301      * is supplied by the return value of the filter.
5302      * <p>
5303      * In all cases, {@code pos} must be greater than or equal to zero, and
5304      * {@code pos} must also be less than or equal to the target's arity.
5305      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5306      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5307 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5308 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5309 ...
5310 MethodHandle deepToString = publicLookup()
5311   .findStatic(Arrays.class, "deepToString", methodType(String.class, Object[].class));
5312 
5313 MethodHandle ts1 = deepToString.asCollector(String[].class, 1);
5314 assertEquals("[strange]", (String) ts1.invokeExact("strange"));
5315 
5316 MethodHandle ts2 = deepToString.asCollector(String[].class, 2);
5317 assertEquals("[up, down]", (String) ts2.invokeExact("up", "down"));
5318 
5319 MethodHandle ts3 = deepToString.asCollector(String[].class, 3);
5320 MethodHandle ts3_ts2 = collectArguments(ts3, 1, ts2);
5321 assertEquals("[top, [up, down], strange]",
5322              (String) ts3_ts2.invokeExact("top", "up", "down", "strange"));
5323 
5324 MethodHandle ts3_ts2_ts1 = collectArguments(ts3_ts2, 3, ts1);
5325 assertEquals("[top, [up, down], [strange]]",
5326              (String) ts3_ts2_ts1.invokeExact("top", "up", "down", "strange"));
5327 
5328 MethodHandle ts3_ts2_ts3 = collectArguments(ts3_ts2, 1, ts3);
5329 assertEquals("[top, [[up, down, strange], charm], bottom]",
5330              (String) ts3_ts2_ts3.invokeExact("top", "up", "down", "strange", "charm", "bottom"));
5331      * }</pre></blockquote>
5332      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5333      * represents the return type of the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5334      * {@code V}/{@code v} stand for the return type and value of the
5335      * {@code filter}, which are also found in the signature and arguments of
5336      * the {@code target}, respectively, unless {@code V} is {@code void}.
5337      * {@code A}/{@code a} and {@code C}/{@code c} represent the parameter types
5338      * and values preceding and following the collection position, {@code pos},
5339      * in the {@code target}'s signature. They also turn up in the resulting
5340      * adapter's signature and arguments, where they surround
5341      * {@code B}/{@code b}, which represent the parameter types and arguments
5342      * to the {@code filter} (if any).
5343      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5344      * T target(A...,V,C...);
5345      * V filter(B...);
5346      * T adapter(A... a,B... b,C... c) {
5347      *   V v = filter(b...);
5348      *   return target(a...,v,c...);
5349      * }
5350      * // and if the filter has no arguments:
5351      * T target2(A...,V,C...);
5352      * V filter2();
5353      * T adapter2(A... a,C... c) {
5354      *   V v = filter2();
5355      *   return target2(a...,v,c...);
5356      * }
5357      * // and if the filter has a void return:
5358      * T target3(A...,C...);
5359      * void filter3(B...);
5360      * T adapter3(A... a,B... b,C... c) {
5361      *   filter3(b...);
5362      *   return target3(a...,c...);
5363      * }
5364      * }</pre></blockquote>
5365      * <p>
5366      * A collection adapter {@code collectArguments(mh, 0, coll)} is equivalent to
5367      * one which first "folds" the affected arguments, and then drops them, in separate
5368      * steps as follows:
5369      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5370      * mh = MethodHandles.dropArguments(mh, 1, coll.type().parameterList()); //step 2
5371      * mh = MethodHandles.foldArguments(mh, coll); //step 1
5372      * }</pre></blockquote>
5373      * If the target method handle consumes no arguments besides than the result
5374      * (if any) of the filter {@code coll}, then {@code collectArguments(mh, 0, coll)}
5375      * is equivalent to {@code filterReturnValue(coll, mh)}.
5376      * If the filter method handle {@code coll} consumes one argument and produces
5377      * a non-void result, then {@code collectArguments(mh, N, coll)}
5378      * is equivalent to {@code filterArguments(mh, N, coll)}.
5379      * Other equivalences are possible but would require argument permutation.
5380      * <p>
5381      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5382      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5383      *
5384      * @param target the method handle to invoke after filtering the subsequence of arguments
5385      * @param pos the position of the first adapter argument to pass to the filter,
5386      *            and/or the target argument which receives the result of the filter
5387      * @param filter method handle to call on the subsequence of arguments
5388      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument subsequence filtering logic
5389      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5390      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the return type of {@code filter}
5391      *          is non-void and is not the same as the {@code pos} argument of the target,
5392      *          or if {@code pos} is not between 0 and the target's arity, inclusive,
5393      *          or if the resulting method handle's type would have
5394      *          <a href="MethodHandle.html#maxarity">too many parameters</a>
5395      * @see MethodHandles#foldArguments
5396      * @see MethodHandles#filterArguments
5397      * @see MethodHandles#filterReturnValue
5398      */
5399     public static MethodHandle collectArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) {
5400         MethodType newType = collectArgumentsChecks(target, pos, filter);
5401         MethodType collectorType = filter.type();
5402         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5403         LambdaForm lform;
5404         if (collectorType.returnType().isArray() && filter.intrinsicName() == Intrinsic.NEW_ARRAY) {
5405             lform = result.editor().collectArgumentArrayForm(1 + pos, filter);
5406             if (lform != null) {
5407                 return result.copyWith(newType, lform);
5408             }
5409         }
5410         lform = result.editor().collectArgumentsForm(1 + pos, collectorType.basicType());
5411         return result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5412     }
5413 
5414     private static MethodType collectArgumentsChecks(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle filter) throws RuntimeException {
5415         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5416         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5417         Class<?> rtype = filterType.returnType();
5418         List<Class<?>> filterArgs = filterType.parameterList();
5419         if (rtype == void.class) {
5420             return targetType.insertParameterTypes(pos, filterArgs);
5421         }
5422         if (rtype != targetType.parameterType(pos)) {
5423             throw newIllegalArgumentException("target and filter types do not match", targetType, filterType);
5424         }
5425         return targetType.dropParameterTypes(pos, pos+1).insertParameterTypes(pos, filterArgs);
5426     }
5427 
5428     /**
5429      * Adapts a target method handle by post-processing
5430      * its return value (if any) with a filter (another method handle).
5431      * The result of the filter is returned from the adapter.
5432      * <p>
5433      * If the target returns a value, the filter must accept that value as
5434      * its only argument.
5435      * If the target returns void, the filter must accept no arguments.
5436      * <p>
5437      * The return type of the filter
5438      * replaces the return type of the target
5439      * in the resulting adapted method handle.
5440      * The argument type of the filter (if any) must be identical to the
5441      * return type of the target.
5442      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5443      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5444 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5445 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5446 ...
5447 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5448   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5449 MethodHandle length = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5450   "length", methodType(int.class));
5451 System.out.println((String) cat.invokeExact("x", "y")); // xy
5452 MethodHandle f0 = filterReturnValue(cat, length);
5453 System.out.println((int) f0.invokeExact("x", "y")); // 2
5454      * }</pre></blockquote>
5455      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code,
5456      * {@code T}/{@code t} represent the result type and value of the
5457      * {@code target}; {@code V}, the result type of the {@code filter}; and
5458      * {@code A}/{@code a}, the types and values of the parameters and arguments
5459      * of the {@code target} as well as the resulting adapter.
5460      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5461      * T target(A...);
5462      * V filter(T);
5463      * V adapter(A... a) {
5464      *   T t = target(a...);
5465      *   return filter(t);
5466      * }
5467      * // and if the target has a void return:
5468      * void target2(A...);
5469      * V filter2();
5470      * V adapter2(A... a) {
5471      *   target2(a...);
5472      *   return filter2();
5473      * }
5474      * // and if the filter has a void return:
5475      * T target3(A...);
5476      * void filter3(V);
5477      * void adapter3(A... a) {
5478      *   T t = target3(a...);
5479      *   filter3(t);
5480      * }
5481      * }</pre></blockquote>
5482      * <p>
5483      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5484      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5485      * @param target the method handle to invoke before filtering the return value
5486      * @param filter method handle to call on the return value
5487      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified return value filtering logic
5488      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5489      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the argument list of {@code filter}
5490      *          does not match the return type of target as described above
5491      */
5492     public static MethodHandle filterReturnValue(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle filter) {
5493         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5494         MethodType filterType = filter.type();
5495         filterReturnValueChecks(targetType, filterType);
5496         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5497         BasicType rtype = BasicType.basicType(filterType.returnType());
5498         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().filterReturnForm(rtype, false);
5499         MethodType newType = targetType.changeReturnType(filterType.returnType());
5500         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, filter);
5501         return result;
5502     }
5503 
5504     private static void filterReturnValueChecks(MethodType targetType, MethodType filterType) throws RuntimeException {
5505         Class<?> rtype = targetType.returnType();
5506         int filterValues = filterType.parameterCount();
5507         if (filterValues == 0
5508                 ? (rtype != void.class)
5509                 : (rtype != filterType.parameterType(0) || filterValues != 1))
5510             throw newIllegalArgumentException("target and filter types do not match", targetType, filterType);
5511     }
5512 
5513     /**
5514      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing
5515      * some of its arguments, and then calling the target with
5516      * the result of the pre-processing, inserted into the original
5517      * sequence of arguments.
5518      * <p>
5519      * The pre-processing is performed by {@code combiner}, a second method handle.
5520      * Of the arguments passed to the adapter, the first {@code N} arguments
5521      * are copied to the combiner, which is then called.
5522      * (Here, {@code N} is defined as the parameter count of the combiner.)
5523      * After this, control passes to the target, with any result
5524      * from the combiner inserted before the original {@code N} incoming
5525      * arguments.
5526      * <p>
5527      * If the combiner returns a value, the first parameter type of the target
5528      * must be identical with the return type of the combiner, and the next
5529      * {@code N} parameter types of the target must exactly match the parameters
5530      * of the combiner.
5531      * <p>
5532      * If the combiner has a void return, no result will be inserted,
5533      * and the first {@code N} parameter types of the target
5534      * must exactly match the parameters of the combiner.
5535      * <p>
5536      * The resulting adapter is the same type as the target, except that the
5537      * first parameter type is dropped,
5538      * if it corresponds to the result of the combiner.
5539      * <p>
5540      * (Note that {@link #dropArguments(MethodHandle,int,List) dropArguments} can be used to remove any arguments
5541      * that either the combiner or the target does not wish to receive.
5542      * If some of the incoming arguments are destined only for the combiner,
5543      * consider using {@link MethodHandle#asCollector asCollector} instead, since those
5544      * arguments will not need to be live on the stack on entry to the
5545      * target.)
5546      * <p><b>Example:</b>
5547      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5548 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5549 import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5550 ...
5551 MethodHandle trace = publicLookup().findVirtual(java.io.PrintStream.class,
5552   "println", methodType(void.class, String.class))
5553     .bindTo(System.out);
5554 MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5555   "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5556 assertEquals("boojum", (String) cat.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5557 MethodHandle catTrace = foldArguments(cat, trace);
5558 // also prints "boo":
5559 assertEquals("boojum", (String) catTrace.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5560      * }</pre></blockquote>
5561      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5562      * represents the result type of the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5563      * {@code V}/{@code v} represent the type and value of the parameter and argument
5564      * of {@code target} that precedes the folding position; {@code V} also is
5565      * the result type of the {@code combiner}. {@code A}/{@code a} denote the
5566      * types and values of the {@code N} parameters and arguments at the folding
5567      * position. {@code B}/{@code b} represent the types and values of the
5568      * {@code target} parameters and arguments that follow the folded parameters
5569      * and arguments.
5570      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5571      * // there are N arguments in A...
5572      * T target(V, A[N]..., B...);
5573      * V combiner(A...);
5574      * T adapter(A... a, B... b) {
5575      *   V v = combiner(a...);
5576      *   return target(v, a..., b...);
5577      * }
5578      * // and if the combiner has a void return:
5579      * T target2(A[N]..., B...);
5580      * void combiner2(A...);
5581      * T adapter2(A... a, B... b) {
5582      *   combiner2(a...);
5583      *   return target2(a..., b...);
5584      * }
5585      * }</pre></blockquote>
5586      * <p>
5587      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5588      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5589      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5590      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5591      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5592      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5593      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code combiner}'s return type
5594      *          is non-void and not the same as the first argument type of
5595      *          the target, or if the initial {@code N} argument types
5596      *          of the target
5597      *          (skipping one matching the {@code combiner}'s return type)
5598      *          are not identical with the argument types of {@code combiner}
5599      */
5600     public static MethodHandle foldArguments(MethodHandle target, MethodHandle combiner) {
5601         return foldArguments(target, 0, combiner);
5602     }
5603 
5604     /**
5605      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing some of its arguments, starting at a given position, and then
5606      * calling the target with the result of the pre-processing, inserted into the original sequence of arguments just
5607      * before the folded arguments.
5608      * <p>
5609      * This method is closely related to {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}, but allows to control the
5610      * position in the parameter list at which folding takes place. The argument controlling this, {@code pos}, is a
5611      * zero-based index. The aforementioned method {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)} assumes position
5612      * 0.
5613      *
5614      * @apiNote Example:
5615      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5616     import static java.lang.invoke.MethodHandles.*;
5617     import static java.lang.invoke.MethodType.*;
5618     ...
5619     MethodHandle trace = publicLookup().findVirtual(java.io.PrintStream.class,
5620     "println", methodType(void.class, String.class))
5621     .bindTo(System.out);
5622     MethodHandle cat = lookup().findVirtual(String.class,
5623     "concat", methodType(String.class, String.class));
5624     assertEquals("boojum", (String) cat.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5625     MethodHandle catTrace = foldArguments(cat, 1, trace);
5626     // also prints "jum":
5627     assertEquals("boojum", (String) catTrace.invokeExact("boo", "jum"));
5628      * }</pre></blockquote>
5629      * <p>Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5630      * represents the result type of the {@code target} and resulting adapter.
5631      * {@code V}/{@code v} represent the type and value of the parameter and argument
5632      * of {@code target} that precedes the folding position; {@code V} also is
5633      * the result type of the {@code combiner}. {@code A}/{@code a} denote the
5634      * types and values of the {@code N} parameters and arguments at the folding
5635      * position. {@code Z}/{@code z} and {@code B}/{@code b} represent the types
5636      * and values of the {@code target} parameters and arguments that precede and
5637      * follow the folded parameters and arguments starting at {@code pos},
5638      * respectively.
5639      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5640      * // there are N arguments in A...
5641      * T target(Z..., V, A[N]..., B...);
5642      * V combiner(A...);
5643      * T adapter(Z... z, A... a, B... b) {
5644      *   V v = combiner(a...);
5645      *   return target(z..., v, a..., b...);
5646      * }
5647      * // and if the combiner has a void return:
5648      * T target2(Z..., A[N]..., B...);
5649      * void combiner2(A...);
5650      * T adapter2(Z... z, A... a, B... b) {
5651      *   combiner2(a...);
5652      *   return target2(z..., a..., b...);
5653      * }
5654      * }</pre></blockquote>
5655      * <p>
5656      * <em>Note:</em> The resulting adapter is never a {@linkplain MethodHandle#asVarargsCollector
5657      * variable-arity method handle}, even if the original target method handle was.
5658      *
5659      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5660      * @param pos the position at which to start folding and at which to insert the folding result; if this is {@code
5661      *            0}, the effect is the same as for {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}.
5662      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5663      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5664      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5665      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if either of the following two conditions holds:
5666      *          (1) {@code combiner}'s return type is non-{@code void} and not the same as the argument type at position
5667      *              {@code pos} of the target signature;
5668      *          (2) the {@code N} argument types at position {@code pos} of the target signature (skipping one matching
5669      *              the {@code combiner}'s return type) are not identical with the argument types of {@code combiner}.
5670      *
5671      * @see #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)
5672      * @since 9
5673      */
5674     public static MethodHandle foldArguments(MethodHandle target, int pos, MethodHandle combiner) {
5675         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5676         MethodType combinerType = combiner.type();
5677         Class<?> rtype = foldArgumentChecks(pos, targetType, combinerType);
5678         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5679         boolean dropResult = rtype == void.class;
5680         LambdaForm lform = result.editor().foldArgumentsForm(1 + pos, dropResult, combinerType.basicType());
5681         MethodType newType = targetType;
5682         if (!dropResult) {
5683             newType = newType.dropParameterTypes(pos, pos + 1);
5684         }
5685         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, combiner);
5686         return result;
5687     }
5688 
5689     private static Class<?> foldArgumentChecks(int foldPos, MethodType targetType, MethodType combinerType) {
5690         int foldArgs   = combinerType.parameterCount();
5691         Class<?> rtype = combinerType.returnType();
5692         int foldVals = rtype == void.class ? 0 : 1;
5693         int afterInsertPos = foldPos + foldVals;
5694         boolean ok = (targetType.parameterCount() >= afterInsertPos + foldArgs);
5695         if (ok) {
5696             for (int i = 0; i < foldArgs; i++) {
5697                 if (combinerType.parameterType(i) != targetType.parameterType(i + afterInsertPos)) {
5698                     ok = false;
5699                     break;
5700                 }
5701             }
5702         }
5703         if (ok && foldVals != 0 && combinerType.returnType() != targetType.parameterType(foldPos))
5704             ok = false;
5705         if (!ok)
5706             throw misMatchedTypes("target and combiner types", targetType, combinerType);
5707         return rtype;
5708     }
5709 
5710     /**
5711      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing some of its arguments, then calling the target with the result
5712      * of the pre-processing replacing the argument at the given position.
5713      *
5714      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5715      * @param position the position at which to start folding and at which to insert the folding result; if this is {@code
5716      *            0}, the effect is the same as for {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}.
5717      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5718      * @param argPositions indexes of the target to pick arguments sent to the combiner from
5719      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5720      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5721      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if either of the following two conditions holds:
5722      *          (1) {@code combiner}'s return type is not the same as the argument type at position
5723      *              {@code pos} of the target signature;
5724      *          (2) the {@code N} argument types at positions {@code argPositions[1...N]} of the target signature are
5725      *              not identical with the argument types of {@code combiner}.
5726      */
5727     /*non-public*/
5728     static MethodHandle filterArgumentsWithCombiner(MethodHandle target, int position, MethodHandle combiner, int ... argPositions) {
5729         return argumentsWithCombiner(true, target, position, combiner, argPositions);
5730     }
5731 
5732     /**
5733      * Adapts a target method handle by pre-processing some of its arguments, calling the target with the result of
5734      * the pre-processing inserted into the original sequence of arguments at the given position.
5735      *
5736      * @param target the method handle to invoke after arguments are combined
5737      * @param position the position at which to start folding and at which to insert the folding result; if this is {@code
5738      *            0}, the effect is the same as for {@link #foldArguments(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)}.
5739      * @param combiner method handle to call initially on the incoming arguments
5740      * @param argPositions indexes of the target to pick arguments sent to the combiner from
5741      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified argument folding logic
5742      * @throws NullPointerException if either argument is null
5743      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if either of the following two conditions holds:
5744      *          (1) {@code combiner}'s return type is non-{@code void} and not the same as the argument type at position
5745      *              {@code pos} of the target signature;
5746      *          (2) the {@code N} argument types at positions {@code argPositions[1...N]} of the target signature
5747      *              (skipping {@code position} where the {@code combiner}'s return will be folded in) are not identical
5748      *              with the argument types of {@code combiner}.
5749      */
5750     /*non-public*/
5751     static MethodHandle foldArgumentsWithCombiner(MethodHandle target, int position, MethodHandle combiner, int ... argPositions) {
5752         return argumentsWithCombiner(false, target, position, combiner, argPositions);
5753     }
5754 
5755     private static MethodHandle argumentsWithCombiner(boolean filter, MethodHandle target, int position, MethodHandle combiner, int ... argPositions) {
5756         MethodType targetType = target.type();
5757         MethodType combinerType = combiner.type();
5758         Class<?> rtype = argumentsWithCombinerChecks(position, filter, targetType, combinerType, argPositions);
5759         BoundMethodHandle result = target.rebind();
5760 
5761         MethodType newType = targetType;
5762         LambdaForm lform;
5763         if (filter) {
5764             lform = result.editor().filterArgumentsForm(1 + position, combinerType.basicType(), argPositions);
5765         } else {
5766             boolean dropResult = rtype == void.class;
5767             lform = result.editor().foldArgumentsForm(1 + position, dropResult, combinerType.basicType(), argPositions);
5768             if (!dropResult) {
5769                 newType = newType.dropParameterTypes(position, position + 1);
5770             }
5771         }
5772         result = result.copyWithExtendL(newType, lform, combiner);
5773         return result;
5774     }
5775 
5776     private static Class<?> argumentsWithCombinerChecks(int position, boolean filter, MethodType targetType, MethodType combinerType, int ... argPos) {
5777         int combinerArgs = combinerType.parameterCount();
5778         if (argPos.length != combinerArgs) {
5779             throw newIllegalArgumentException("combiner and argument map must be equal size", combinerType, argPos.length);
5780         }
5781         Class<?> rtype = combinerType.returnType();
5782 
5783         for (int i = 0; i < combinerArgs; i++) {
5784             int arg = argPos[i];
5785             if (arg < 0 || arg > targetType.parameterCount()) {
5786                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("arg outside of target parameterRange", targetType, arg);
5787             }
5788             if (combinerType.parameterType(i) != targetType.parameterType(arg)) {
5789                 throw newIllegalArgumentException("target argument type at position " + arg
5790                         + " must match combiner argument type at index " + i + ": " + targetType
5791                         + " -> " + combinerType + ", map: " + Arrays.toString(argPos));
5792             }
5793         }
5794         if (filter && combinerType.returnType() != targetType.parameterType(position)) {
5795             throw misMatchedTypes("target and combiner types", targetType, combinerType);
5796         }
5797         return rtype;
5798     }
5799 
5800     /**
5801      * Makes a method handle which adapts a target method handle,
5802      * by guarding it with a test, a boolean-valued method handle.
5803      * If the guard fails, a fallback handle is called instead.
5804      * All three method handles must have the same corresponding
5805      * argument and return types, except that the return type
5806      * of the test must be boolean, and the test is allowed
5807      * to have fewer arguments than the other two method handles.
5808      * <p>
5809      * Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5810      * represents the uniform result type of the three involved handles;
5811      * {@code A}/{@code a}, the types and values of the {@code target}
5812      * parameters and arguments that are consumed by the {@code test}; and
5813      * {@code B}/{@code b}, those types and values of the {@code target}
5814      * parameters and arguments that are not consumed by the {@code test}.
5815      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5816      * boolean test(A...);
5817      * T target(A...,B...);
5818      * T fallback(A...,B...);
5819      * T adapter(A... a,B... b) {
5820      *   if (test(a...))
5821      *     return target(a..., b...);
5822      *   else
5823      *     return fallback(a..., b...);
5824      * }
5825      * }</pre></blockquote>
5826      * Note that the test arguments ({@code a...} in the pseudocode) cannot
5827      * be modified by execution of the test, and so are passed unchanged
5828      * from the caller to the target or fallback as appropriate.
5829      * @param test method handle used for test, must return boolean
5830      * @param target method handle to call if test passes
5831      * @param fallback method handle to call if test fails
5832      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified if/then/else logic
5833      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
5834      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code test} does not return boolean,
5835      *          or if all three method types do not match (with the return
5836      *          type of {@code test} changed to match that of the target).
5837      */
5838     public static MethodHandle guardWithTest(MethodHandle test,
5839                                MethodHandle target,
5840                                MethodHandle fallback) {
5841         MethodType gtype = test.type();
5842         MethodType ttype = target.type();
5843         MethodType ftype = fallback.type();
5844         if (!ttype.equals(ftype))
5845             throw misMatchedTypes("target and fallback types", ttype, ftype);
5846         if (gtype.returnType() != boolean.class)
5847             throw newIllegalArgumentException("guard type is not a predicate "+gtype);
5848         List<Class<?>> targs = ttype.parameterList();
5849         test = dropArgumentsToMatch(test, 0, targs, 0, true);
5850         if (test == null) {
5851             throw misMatchedTypes("target and test types", ttype, gtype);
5852         }
5853         return MethodHandleImpl.makeGuardWithTest(test, target, fallback);
5854     }
5855 
5856     static <T> RuntimeException misMatchedTypes(String what, T t1, T t2) {
5857         return newIllegalArgumentException(what + " must match: " + t1 + " != " + t2);
5858     }
5859 
5860     /**
5861      * Makes a method handle which adapts a target method handle,
5862      * by running it inside an exception handler.
5863      * If the target returns normally, the adapter returns that value.
5864      * If an exception matching the specified type is thrown, the fallback
5865      * handle is called instead on the exception, plus the original arguments.
5866      * <p>
5867      * The target and handler must have the same corresponding
5868      * argument and return types, except that handler may omit trailing arguments
5869      * (similarly to the predicate in {@link #guardWithTest guardWithTest}).
5870      * Also, the handler must have an extra leading parameter of {@code exType} or a supertype.
5871      * <p>
5872      * Here is pseudocode for the resulting adapter. In the code, {@code T}
5873      * represents the return type of the {@code target} and {@code handler},
5874      * and correspondingly that of the resulting adapter; {@code A}/{@code a},
5875      * the types and values of arguments to the resulting handle consumed by
5876      * {@code handler}; and {@code B}/{@code b}, those of arguments to the
5877      * resulting handle discarded by {@code handler}.
5878      * <blockquote><pre>{@code
5879      * T target(A..., B...);
5880      * T handler(ExType, A...);
5881      * T adapter(A... a, B... b) {
5882      *   try {
5883      *     return target(a..., b...);
5884      *   } catch (ExType ex) {
5885      *     return handler(ex, a...);
5886      *   }
5887      * }
5888      * }</pre></blockquote>
5889      * Note that the saved arguments ({@code a...} in the pseudocode) cannot
5890      * be modified by execution of the target, and so are passed unchanged
5891      * from the caller to the handler, if the handler is invoked.
5892      * <p>
5893      * The target and handler must return the same type, even if the handler
5894      * always throws.  (This might happen, for instance, because the handler
5895      * is simulating a {@code finally} clause).
5896      * To create such a throwing handler, compose the handler creation logic
5897      * with {@link #throwException throwException},
5898      * in order to create a method handle of the correct return type.
5899      * @param target method handle to call
5900      * @param exType the type of exception which the handler will catch
5901      * @param handler method handle to call if a matching exception is thrown
5902      * @return method handle which incorporates the specified try/catch logic
5903      * @throws NullPointerException if any argument is null
5904      * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code handler} does not accept
5905      *          the given exception type, or if the method handle types do
5906      *          not match in their return types and their
5907      *          corresponding parameters
5908      * @see MethodHandles#tryFinally(MethodHandle, MethodHandle)
5909      */
5910     public static MethodHandle catchException(MethodHandle target,
